    //         //   after each year is calculated,  put the star for that year in pickyears table
    //         // ===========================================================================================================
    //         gbl_yrfirst = 1978
    //         gbl_yrlast  = 1986
    //         
    //         tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(gbl_yrfirst);  // does FROM gbl_yrfirst TO gbl_yrlast -  current year is arg
    //         
    //         
    //         func tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(arg_yrtodo)
    //         {
    //           ... calc arg_yrtodo
    //         
    //           tg_finishedYear(arg_yrtodo)
    //         }

    //            
    //             // NOTE:
    //             //   before going back to tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(arg_yrtodo) to calculate the next year,
    //             //   allow X ms for the DOM to display the star in the pickyears table
    //             //
    //             // Most everything in the browser stops while a Javascript is running.
    //             // This includes for example DOM rendering, event handling, image animation.
    //             // The only way to cause the DOM to be rendered is to end the Javascript.
    //             // You can use the setTimeout method to start code again after the update:
    //             //
    //             setTimeout(
    //               tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(arg_yrtodo),
    //               50                                // KEY: allow X ms for the DOM to display the star in the table

    //         //   after each year is calculated,  put the star for that year in pickyears table
    //         // ======  STRATEGY  =========================================================================================
    //
    //
    // INSTEAD OF:  doing this simple loop
    //              for ( loopTNyear = arg_yearSTART ;  loopTNyear  <=  arg_yearEND ;    loopTNyear =  parseInt(loopTNyear, 10)  + 1 )    // for each year to do
    //
    // DO THIS:  tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(arg_yearSTART);  // RECURSIVLY  call this fn so DOM rendering of new star for each year has time to happen
    //
function tg_finishedYear()   // rkfns
{
// smup_log('\n\nin function tg_finishedYear()');
     var arg_yrtodo = gbls_TN_yeartodo ;  // current processing year in tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()
// smup_log('arg_yrtodo =[' + arg_yrtodo  + ']');

      var loop2TNyear = arg_yrtodo; 
// smup_log('loop2TNyear  =[' + loop2TNyear   + ']  SET in function tg_finishedYear()');

  //  write star of arg_yrtodo in pickyr table bucket
  //
  // put green stars in   historical comment))
// smup_log('   put green stars in');

//  $('#imgSTARgr2').css('height', (th_starH3 / 2) ).css('width', ( th_starW3 / 2) )
//  $('#imgSTARgr2').css('display','inline-block').css('visibility','visible').clone() .appendTo( $('#PICKyr' + pickYrBucket) );

  // get the star image having the right color 
  //
  var IDcoverStar;
  if (gbls_TG_stressScore >= 90                                ) IDcoverStar = 'imgSTARgr2' ;
  if (gbls_TG_stressScore >= 75  &&  gbls_TG_stressScore <  90 ) IDcoverStar = 'imgSTARgre' ;
  if (gbls_TG_stressScore >  50  &&  gbls_TG_stressScore <  75 ) IDcoverStar = 'imgSTARneu' ;
  if (gbls_TG_stressScore >  25  &&  gbls_TG_stressScore <= 50 ) IDcoverStar = 'imgSTARneu' ;
  if (gbls_TG_stressScore >  10  &&  gbls_TG_stressScore <= 25 ) IDcoverStar = 'imgSTARred' ;
  if (                               gbls_TG_stressScore <= 10 ) IDcoverStar = 'imgSTARre2' ;
// smup_log('IDcoverStar =[' + IDcoverStar  + ']');

  // get bucket number in the pickyears table for the current year number the loop is on (loop2TNyear)
  //
  var bktNumForloopTNyear;
  bktNumForloopTNyear = loop2TNyear - gbls_pickyr_first ;   //  year number of first year in pickyr table 
// smup_log('bktNumForloopTNyear =[' + bktNumForloopTNyear  + ']');
// smup_log('loop2TNyear          =[' + loop2TNyear   + ']');
// smup_log('gbls_pickyr_first   =[' + gbls_pickyr_first   + ']');



//  $('#imgSTARgr2').css('height', '34px' ).css('width', '21px' );
//  $('#imgSTARgr2').css('display','inline-block').css('visibility','visible').clone() .appendTo( $('#PICKyrA' + bktNumForloopTNyear ) );



  // remove the first 2 chars of year
  // bgcolor = black
  //
  $('#PICKyr' + gbls_pickyr_AorB  + bktNumForloopTNyear).css('background-color', 'black').text( $('#PICKyr' + bktNumForloopTNyear).text().substring(2) );


  // NOTE: the   .prop('id', IDcoverStar)  below HAS TO BE THERE  or it will not go into the year number div
//  $('#' + IDcoverStar).css('height', gbls_starPikYr_h ).css('width', gbls_starPikYr_w ).css('padding', '3px');
  $('#' + IDcoverStar).css('height', gbls_starPikYr_h ).css('width', gbls_starPikYr_w ).css('padding-left', '3px').css('padding-right', '3px');;

// OLD   no A and B
//  $('#' + IDcoverStar).css('display','inline-block').css('visibility','visible').clone().prop('id', IDcoverStar + bktNumForloopTNyear).appendTo( $('#PICKyr' + bktNumForloopTNyear ) ); // NOTE: the   .prop('id', IDcoverStar)  HAS TO BE THERE  or it will not go into the year number div


  // update both A and B.  Put the current year star into pickyr table 
  //
  // NOTE: the   .prop('id', IDcoverStar)  HAS TO BE THERE  or it will not go into the year number div
  $('#' + IDcoverStar).css('display','inline-block').css('visibility','visible').clone().prop('id', IDcoverStar + 'A' + bktNumForloopTNyear).appendTo( $('#PICKyrA' + bktNumForloopTNyear ) );
//  $('#' + IDcoverStar).css('display','inline-block').css('visibility','visible').clone().prop('id', IDcoverStar + 'B' + bktNumForloopTNyear).appendTo( $('#PICKyrB' + bktNumForloopTNyear ) ); 

  $('#PICKyr' + gbls_pickyr_AorB  + bktNumForloopTNyear)
    .css('padding', '0px')
    .css('margin-right', '3px')
//    .css('margin-right', pad_r + 'px')
//    .css('padding-right', pad_r + 'px')
//    .css('margin-bottom', '-15px')
  ;
  //
  //  write star of arg_yrtodo in pickyr table bucket
//

  
// smup_log('arg_yrtodo           =[' + arg_yrtodo   + ']');
// smup_log('gbls_getTNdataYRend  =[' + gbls_getTNdataYRend   + ']');

  if (arg_yrtodo == gbls_getTNdataYRend )   {
// smup_log('FINISHED function tg_finishedYear()  ALL DONe  AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA\n\n');
    return   // ALL DONE
  }
  else {

    //             // NOTE:
    //             //   before going back to tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(arg_yrtodo) to calculate the next year,
    //             //   allow X ms for the DOM to display the star in the pickyears table
    //             //
    //             // Most everything in the browser stops while a Javascript is running.
    //             // This includes for example DOM rendering, event handling, image animation.
    //             // The only way to cause the DOM to be rendered is to end the Javascript.
    //             // You can use the setTimeout method to start code again after the update:
    //             //
    //             setTimeout(
    //               tg_doYearsOneAtAtime(arg_yrtodo),
    //               50                                // KEY: allow X ms for the DOM to display the star in the table
    //             );
    //
    arg_yrtodo = (arg_yrtodo * 1) + 1 ; // star 1  makes it a number and  not string

    gbls_TN_yeartodo = arg_yrtodo ;  // current processing year in tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()

// smup_log('arg_yrtodo  =[' + arg_yrtodo   + ']');
// smup_log('FINISHED function tg_finishedYear  INCREMENTED gbls_TN_yeartodo BEFORE settimeout  \n\n');
// smup_log('line before settimeout call tg_doYearsOneAtAtime');

    // KEY: allow X ms for the DOM to display the star in the table

//
//// is arg a prob ?
//    setTimeout( function() {
//        tg_doYearsOneAtAtime() ;    // gbls_TN_yeartodo  ;  // current processing year in tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()
//      },
//      500
//    );
//

setTimeout( function() {
//       try              setTimeout(newNumber, 1);    // ONE ms !!
//    setTimeout(tg_doYearsOneAtAtime, 1);
    setTimeout(tg_doYearsOneAtAtime, 20);
//    setTimeout(tg_doYearsOneAtAtime, 7);
//    tg_doYearsOneAtAtime();
//    setTimeout(tg_doYearsOneAtAtime, 1000);
      },
      50
    );
  }


} // end of function tg_finishedYear(arg_yrtodo) 


// RECURSIVLY  call this fn so DOM rendering of new star for each year has time to happen
function tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()   // rkfns
{
smup_log('\n\nin function tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()');
smup_log('getDateMS() =[' + getDateMS()  + ']');


//  // for test
//gbls_tmpdb = gbls_tmpdb + 1 ;
//if(gbls_tmpdb >= 5) return;


    // yyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyy
//    for ( loopTNyear = arg_yearSTART ;  loopTNyear  <=  arg_yearEND ;    loopTNyear =  parseInt(loopTNyear, 10)  + 1 )    // for each year to do

      var arg_yeartodo = gbls_TN_yeartodo ;  // (no more args)  current processing year in tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()
smup_log('arg_yeartodo =[' + arg_yeartodo  + ']');
      var loopTNyear   = arg_yeartodo; 
smup_log('loopTNyear  =[' + loopTNyear   + ']  SET in function tg_doYearsOneAtAtime()');

      var id_ofThumbnail_data  = '';
      var divNumberString      = '';    // "03", "24" ...

      gbls_dob_ctr = gbls_dob_ctr + 1;  // 0 => year of birth
  //smup_log('gbls_dob_ctr       =[' + gbls_dob_ctr   + ']');
  //smup_log('loopTNyear  =[' + loopTNyear   + ']');

      // 1.  for each year,   get data for building the thumbnail and put it in gbls_text_DATA_for_tg
      // 1.  for each year,   get data for building the thumbnail and put it in gbls_text_DATA_for_tg
      //

//smup_log('loopTNyear           0 =[' + loopTNyear  + ']');
//      var tstType63 = typeof loopTNyear;
//smup_log('tstType63  loopTNyear  0 =[' + tstType63   + ']');


      // STRANGE   here   emscripten  treats a js arg containing "2018" as a number and we get value "" in C
      // MUST force arg to be a STRING
      // + "" forces arg to be a STRING
      // THEN in C you get "2018"  instead of ""
      //
      var yyyy_argAsString2 = loopTNyear + "" ;  // + "" forces arg to be a STRING
  //smup_log('yyyy_argAsString2             1 =[' + yyyy_argAsString2   + ']');
//        var tstType62 = typeof yyyy_argAsString2;
//smup_log('tstType62  yyyy_argAsString2    0 =[' + tstType62   + ']');

      gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg = '\0'.repeat(1024 * gbls_numK_for_tg - 1);  //  (-1 for \0)

      // smup // Write the string to memory
      //
      var Module = {};  // see comment  MODULE MAGIC 

//      Module.stringToUTF8(gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg, gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg, gbls_numK_for_tg * 1024);
      stringToUTF8(gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg, gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg, gbls_numK_for_tg * 1024);

      // smup // We can now send gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg into a C function, it is just a normal char* pointer


                    // LS LOCAL STORAGE LS
                    //
                    // Note: Name/value pairs are always stored as strings. Remember to convert them to another format when needed!
                    // Store        localStorage.setItem("lastname", "Smith");
                    // Retrieve     localStorage.getItem("lastname");                document.getElementById("result").innerHTML = localStorage.getItem("lastname");
                    // Remove       localStorage.removeItem("lastname");             removing the "lastname" localStorage item
                    //
                    // LOCAL STORAGE


      // here we get the thumbnail data by
      // 1. retreiving it from the cache (gbls_TN_data)   (fast)
      // 2. running the C program to calculate it         (about 1/2 second)
      //

  //    if (gbls_TNsALLinCache  == 'yes')
      if (gbls_cache_UseExisting  == 'yes')
      {
  smup_log('WW here we get the thumbnail data by  1. retreiving it from the cache (gbls_TN_data)   (fast)');

         var numTNs0            = gbls_TN_data.length; 
         var arr_TNyearToTest_S = loopTNyear;            
         var arr_TNyearToTest_I = parseInt(loopTNyear,10);
         var TN_currElt         = 'none';
         var TN_searchFor       = 'none';
         var TN_indexOf         = -99;
         var TN_dataParts       = 'none'; 

        for (var i=0; i < numTNs0; i++) {

          TN_currElt   = gbls_TN_data[i];               // TN_currElt is like this  [Justin Bieber|2000|23|Bb8ZZZBb8ZZZBb8ZZZB2fG02B87ZZZB ... ]

          TN_searchFor = gbls_personName_curr + '|' + arr_TNyearToTest_S ;
          TN_indexOf   = gbls_TN_data[i].indexOf(TN_searchFor);     // indexOf('xxx') == 0 (true)  SAME AS   .startsWith('xxx') (true)

  //smup_log('TN_currElt first 51 =[' + TN_currElt.substring(0,50) + ']  ..................................  ');

          if (TN_indexOf != 0) continue;  // this array element is not for gbls_personName_curr 
            // here we found our gbls_TN_data rec
  //smup_log('          WW here we found our gbls_TN_data rec');
            TN_dataParts = TN_currElt.split('|');       // TN_currElt is like this  [Justin Bieber|2000|23|Bb8ZZZBb8ZZZBb8ZZZB2fG02B87ZZZB ... ]

            gbls_text_DATA_for_tg = TN_dataParts[3] ;   // TN_currElt is like this  [Justin Bieber|2000|23|Bb8ZZZBb8ZZZBb8ZZZB2fG02B87ZZZB ... ]
          break;
        }
      }


  //    if (gbls_TNsALLinCache  == 'no')
      if (gbls_cache_UseExisting == 'no')
      {

  //smup_log('WW here we get the thumbnail data by  2. running the C program to calculate it         (about 1/2 second)');
  //smup_log('gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg.length =[' + gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg.length  + ']');


        //  from click in homp person  var csv_person_string   = make_birth_specs_string();  // uses gbls_homp_psv  to create  gbls_ccall_csv1 and return val it

        //  gbls_ccall_csv1 where from  = make_birth_specs_string();  // uses gbls_homp_psv  to create  gbls_ccall_csv1 and return val it

        //  CALC THUMBNAIL
//        gbls_text_DATA_for_tg  = Module.ccall lp 'mamb_report_big_year' ,     // gbls_text_DATA_for_tg   this text data get converted to a canvas graph
        gbls_text_DATA_for_tg  = ccall( 'mamb_report_big_year' ,     // gbls_text_DATA_for_tg   this text data gets converted to a canvas graph
          'string',                                                         // return type
          [ 'string', 'string', 'string', 'string', 'string', 'string' ],   // array of argument types
          [ 'notused',
            gbls_work_space_for_DATA_tg,
            gbls_ccall_csv1,
            yyyy_argAsString2,
            'return only thumbnail data',                       // char *instructions,  /* like  "return only year stress score" */
            'notused'                        // ,stringBuffForStressScore      // not used in this call  (year stess score only)
          ] // array of arguments
        );
        //  CALC THUMBNAIL

  //smup_log('gbls_csv_person_stringTG =[' + gbls_csv_person_stringTG  + ']');
  //smup_log('gbls_ccall_csv1          =[' + gbls_ccall_csv1 + ']');
  smup_log('gbls_text_DATA_for_tg   =[' + gbls_text_DATA_for_tg.substring(0,50) + '] ... [' + gbls_text_DATA_for_tg.substr(-12,12) + ']');  // first 51, last 12

//alert('hey gbls_text_DATA_for_tg1 ');

        // possibly populate ALL TNs in gbls_TN_data for this person
        //

////      //  15px  =  530 px high   510px
////      //  16px  =  560 px high 
////      //  20px  =  725 px high
////      //  30px  = 1100 px high    
////      // 
////      //   apparent rule:
////      //  each 1px increase in font-size gives 40px increase in HTML GRAPH height regardless of pixel size
////      //  there are 57 lines
////      //  at font-size 30px  HTML GRAPH is 1100 px high 
////
////      //   40px increase for 57 lines
////      //   40px increase for  1 lines
////  // fs = 10px  H =  335 for 57 lines   H per line =  5.87 px
////  // fs = 30px  H = 1100 for 57 lines   H per line = 19.37 px
////      //   each 1px increase in font-size gives 40px increase in HTML GRAPH height regardless of pixel size
////      //    
////      //    
////      var scrollingGraphFontSize = '10';
////      var heightAvailForGraph    = 0;
////      var pixelsBeyond_10        = 0;
////      var pixelsPerFontSize      = 40;
////      heightAvailForGraph    = gbls_screenHeight - gbls_underNAVB_height ;   
////      pixelsBeyond_10        = heightAvailForGraph / 40;
////  //    scrollingGraphFontSize = 10 + pixelsBeyond_10 ;
////      scrollingGraphFontSize =    + pixelsBeyond_10 ;
////
////      var desiredHeightPerLine = heightAvailForGraph /  gbls_TNnumLines ;
////
////      // fs = 10 px   H per line =  5.87 px
////      // fs = 30 px   H per line = 19.37 px
////      // fs increase of 20 px  gives H per line increase of  13.5   px
////      // fs increase of  1 px  gives H per line increase of   0.67  px
////      // IF desiredHeightPerLine = 21
////      // start from H per line of 5.87 px for fs = 10px
////      // keep adding 1px fontsize ( 0.67 px H per line increase )
////      //   until we get to desiredHeightPerLine 
////      var fontSizeCtr = 10;
////  smup_log('---------------------------------');
////  smup_log('gbls_screenHeight      =[' + gbls_screenHeight   + ']');
////  smup_log('gbls_underNAVB_height  =[' + gbls_underNAVB_height   + ']');
////  smup_log('heightAvailForGraph    =[' + heightAvailForGraph   + ']');
////  smup_log('gbls_TNnumLines        =[' + gbls_TNnumLines  + ']');
////  //smup_log('pixelsBeyond_10        =[' + pixelsBeyond_10       + ']');
////  smup_log('desiredHeightPerLine   =[' + desiredHeightPerLine   + ']');
////  smup_log('---------------------------------');
////      for (var hpl = 5.87; (hpl * gbls_TNnumLines) < heightAvailForGraph;  hpl = hpl + 0.67 )  {  // hpl is height per line
////  smup_log('fontSizeCtr  =[' + fontSizeCtr   + ']');
////  smup_log('grh height   =[' + (hpl * gbls_TNnumLines) + ']');
////        fontSizeCtr = fontSizeCtr + 1;
////      }
////      scrollingGraphFontSize = fontSizeCtr - 1;
////  smup_log('scrollingGraphFontSize =[' + scrollingGraphFontSize  + ']');
////
////      if (scrollingGraphFontSize > 12)  scrollingGraphFontSize = 12; 
////
////  smup_log('scrollingGraphFontSize limit size =[' + scrollingGraphFontSize  + ']');
////
////  smup_log('---------------------------------');
////
////      $('#divFUTG').css('font-size', scrollingGraphFontSize + 'px');
////
////      // 
////      // SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT   
////      // SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT    SET HTML GRAPH HEIGHT

if (e.target.id == 'btnNEWGsave' )     // handle click on SAVE button in gDIV_newg
{
  e.stopPropagation(); // Description: Prevents the event from bubbling up the DOM tree, preventing any parent handlers from being notified of the event.

smup_log('CLICK on SAVE button in gDIV_newg');
smup_log('gbls_BEG_EDIT_groupName top of btnNEWGsave=[' + gbls_BEG_EDIT_groupName + ']');
smup_log('gbls_END_EDIT_groupName top of btnNEWGsave=[' + gbls_END_EDIT_groupName + ']');


  // NOTE:  IS func -> e.g. if ( $(this).is('.smupfiller, .smup_highlight_person, .smup_highlight_rptper, .smup_highlight_PIKPper, .smup_highlight_PIKCcity') ) // true if at least one match

//  if ($('#FLD_inputGroupName').is('.placeholderCOLOR') ){rkShowModal( 'myModalNEWG', 'The group name needs to be entered.' );               return; }   // reject SAVE

  var myFLD_inputGroupName = $('#FLD_inputGroupName').val() ;
  if (myFLD_inputGroupName.length == 0)   {rkShowModal( 'myModalNEWG', 'The group name needs to be entered.' );               return; }   // reject SAVE


  // check FLD_inputGroupName for no duplicates
  var LS_record3 = 'none' ;   // LS = Local Storage
    LS_record3 = window.localStorage.getItem(gbls_thisAppTOKEN + gbls_addedGroupTOKEN + myFLD_inputGroupName);  // Retrieve
smup_log('LS_record3 =[' + LS_record3  + ']');

  if (   LS_record3 != null      // local storage record is there => no save
      || myFLD_inputGroupName == 'Example Group'
  )
  {
    rkShowModal( 'myModalNEWG', 'SAME NAME<br>You are trying to save <br>"' + myFLD_inputGroupName + '",<br>but a group with that name exists already.' );
    return;   // reject SAVE
  }


  var myGrpNAME = 'none';
  myGrpNAME = $('#FLD_inputGroupName').val();
  grpDATA_ADD(myGrpNAME);  
//<.> todo
    

  // go back to home from newg
  gbls_routeToHere = 'gHOME_newg' ;
smup_log('CLICK on SAVE button in gDIV_newg');
  showNewScreenOn('CLICK on SAVE button in gDIV_newg');

  return;


} // handle click on SAVE button in gDIV_newg

      //---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      // check if this person is in array gbls_PERlookup
      //---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      found_LSname = 'no';
      for (var i=0; i <= gbls_PERlookup.length - 1; i++) 
      {
        myARRAYname = gbls_PERlookup[i].toString().split('|')[0];   // first field is name ( |-separatged )
//smup_log('check myARRAYname  =[' + myARRAYname   + ']');

        if (myARRAYname == '') 
        {
//smup_log('check if this person is in array gbls_PERlookup');
//smup_log(' GOT myARRAYname  =[' + myARRAYname   + ']');
        }

        if (myARRAYname == myLSname) 
        {
          found_LSname = 'yes';
//smup_log(' FOUND!!! LS person in array gbls_PERlookup');
          break;
        }
      }
      //---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      // check if this person is in array gbls_PERlookup
      //---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

      if (found_LSname == 'yes') {
              // but the jQuery EACH method requires you to use the return statement instead.
              // Return anything that's not false and it will behave as a CONTINUE.
              // Return false, and it will behave as a BREAK:
              //
//smup_log(' FOUND!!! LS person in array gbls_PERlookup goto next LS record\n');
         return 'not false';   // behaves as CONTINUE for jQuery EACH method - see above comment  // Return false, and it will behave as a break:
           // goto next LS record
      }

      if (found_LSname ==  'no') {
smup_log('name not found in gbls_PERlookup array  , SO ADD IT- [' +  myLSname + ']');

        gbls_PERlookup.push( myLSname + '|' + lsvalue);       // <===========  ADD TO array gbls_PERlookup
      }

    } // found a 'smupper' in  localStorage //  localStorage added person (smupper)
